You can enable an out-of-office reply from the Outlook app on your iPhone. Follow the steps below to use this feature.

** NOTE** You will not be able to set a date range (beginning and end date) through the Outlook app.

1. Open your Outlook app and tap the Home icon in the top left.



 


2. Tap the Settings gear icon in the bottom left.



3. Tap your Gresham Smith account. 




 


4. Tap on Automatic Replies. 




 


5. Now toggle Automatic Replies to on and type your message. Tap the check icon in the top right to save and activate your message. When you want to turn it off, return here and toggle it off.

http://aka.ms/ssprsetup

Before you can use the Self-Service Password Reset you need to register for self-service password reset. You can register at http://aka.ms/ssprsetup. You are first required to re-enter your current password.




You will sign in with your company email.




Select Work or School Account.




Enter your current password.




You will need to setup at least 2 of the verification methods listed. Your office phone is not a good option to use if you can't get logged into Teams. The office phone number will be filled in for you. The mobile phone number will be provided if you have your mobile phone listed in the directory. If you set a mobile phone number for verification it will not be listed in the directory. The Authentication email address should not be a gspnet.com or greshamsmith.com number.

Seavus Project Viewer is the only viewer that contains 100% of the viewing functionalities found in Microsoft Project. The viewer will be used to view and print Project files. All computers at Gresham Smith are equipped with this viewer. This will facilitate coordination of project schedules by giving everyone view and print capability. mailto:firstname_lastname@gspnet.com mailto:firstname.lastname@greshamsmith.com https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/How-to-Set-up-the-Authenticator-App%281%29.aspx?List=%7bDFEB7D0D-BA67-4112-A982-964AE1F77471%7d&RootFolder=/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages&ContentTypeId=0x0101009D1CB255DA76424F860D91F20E6C4118003D49C74C4595BD46A27F849EAB9627B2006224A8FFC296244DBDF0491CC92E59D5&Source=https%3a//gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Forms/ByAuthor.aspx

***If you are in the office, you must disconnect your device from wi-fi for initial email setup.***


Configuring email on Android Devices:

 1. On your cell phone, select the Settings icon:





























2. Select Passwords and Accounts: 





























3. Select Add Account:




























4. Select Exchange: 







​​​​​​​
  

 



 



 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 

5. Enter your email address. If you were hired before 4/15/2019, use the firstname_lastname@gspnet.com email format. If you were hired on or after 4/15/2019, use the firstname.lastname@greshamsmith.com email format. Then select Next:




 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 


 

6. Enter your password and select Next:
 


 




 

























7. On the next screen, enter the number shown in the Microsoft Authenticator app to sign in. If you have not set up the Microsoft Authenticator app you can do so here: How to Set Up the Authenticator app Alternatively, you can choose 'I can't use my Microsoft Authenticator app right now' to verify via call or text. 







 





















8. Choose 'text' or 'call' to authenticate:



























9. When your account is verified, select Done. It may be a few minutes before your email fully syncs.

Chats in Teams cannot be deleted, but they can be hidden and unhidden (Although entire chats CANNOT be deleted, you CAN delete individual messages you've sent). Follow the steps below to hide or unhide a chat. 

?

1. Select the chat tab on the left side of the Teams window to view your chats:


 

2. Right-click the chat you would like to hide and click 'Hide'. This will hide your chat.




3. To restore the hidden chat, click in the command bar at the top of the Teams window, search for the person you were chatting with, and select them:





4. Once you again see your chat, right-click it and click 'Unhide'. Your chat will now be unhidden:





?

This article will help you upload a file to a channel in Teams.
 

1. In Microsoft Teams, go to your Channel and click the 'Files' button
 



 



2. From here, you can either click and drag the file into Teams to upload it, or you can click the 'Upload' button
 



 



3. If you clicked the upload button, select the file you'd like to upload and click open





4. You'll see a status icon indicating that your file is uploading. 




5. You'll see your file listed in the Files list when the upload is complete.

Below are steps to help you create a project plan. In Microsoft Project, you can:


 

  • Create project plans.
  • Build project teams and allocate resources.
  • See different views of task and resources.
     
  • Measure progress.
  • Manage budgets.


 

Create a project from a template
 


1. Open Project.

    Or select File > New if you're already working in a project plan.


 

2. Select a template or type in the Search for online templates box and then press Enter.  
 

    Or, choose Blank Project to create a project from scratch.
 


 

3. When you select a template, select the options you want, and select Create.


 

    Change the resources, tasks, and durations in the template so they are right for your project.
 


 

*** Note: To create a new project from an existing project, change the project start and finish dates, and then save the project file with a new name or in a different location. ***

 


Add tasks to a project
 

    1. Select View > Task Views > Gantt Chart?

     2. Type a task name in the first empty Task Name field.

     3. Press Enter.

     4. Repeat steps 2 and 3 to enter the tasks you want.

 




 



 

If adding tasks one at a time starts to take too long, you can also:
 


 

  • Add New Tasks


 

  • Cut and Paste a List from another Program


 

  • Import a Task List from a Sharepoint Site


 

*** For additional resources, please click the links below ***
 

  • Edit a Project


 


  • Manage a Project
     


 


  • Learn More About Project

Follow the steps below to configure the Outlook app for Android. 

1. Open the Google Play store and search for "Outlook" and install the Microsoft Outlook app.

2. Open the Outlook app



3. Click 'Add account' 




4. Enter your email address. If you were hired before 4/15/2019, use firstname_lastname@gspnet.com. If you were hired on or after 4/15/2019, use firstname.lastname@greshamsmith.com. Then click 'Continue'. 

5. If you wish, you can add non-Gresham Smith email accounts to the Outlook app. If not, click 'Maybe later'. 



6. Wait a few moments for your settings to sync. 

7. You'll see a series of informational slides about the Outlook app. Click the arrow to read through these or the Skip button to skip. 

8. Set up is now complete.

There are times when we need to file emails to a specific location due to the need for segregating certain emails from the project shared location. Below are some simple steps to follow when manually filing emails to a specific, non-standard location.

First, we will select the email(s) that we want to file. Be sure when selecting multiples that you are wanting to file these all in the same project. Filing to multiple projects will require multiple manual filings, on a per-project basis. Then, we will click on File in Project button found in the Newforma tool palette.


To find the project you want to file the email in, you can view the My Projects header or My Recent Projects header. If neither of these contain the desired project, then you can select the ellipsis button to the right of the Project field which will launch the Select Project dialog box, as shown below. ​​​​​​​


You can search for your desired project by entering the number or name of the project in the search field, and then clicking the magnifying glass icon immediately to the right. In the example shown, when we put in 19121.00, it returns the project from the All Projects listing that corresponds. Next you will click the OK button at the bottom of the dialog.

The next step is to select Another project location option. The field identifying the alternate location will more than likely appear empty the first time you manually file to this project, as shown below.​​​​​​​

To set this alternate location, click on the ellipsis button to the right of the Another project location field, which will launch the Add to Project Item dialog.  ​​​​​​​

The next step is to click the pull down menu and selecting Project Folders, and then clicking the OK button at the bottom of the dialog box.

This will bring up the listing of folders for the desired project. After selecting the folder, you want to file the email in, click OK at the bottom of the dialog box.

This will take you back to the original File in Project dialog, which will now reflect the choices that you have given it with the previous steps. All that is required to file the email is to click the OK button at the bottom of the dialog, and the filing process will complete.

This procedure gives one common workflow scenario for the entire process of publishing the contents of project folders or document sets to Info Exchange from Project Center so that they can be updated at any time by anyone on the project team. It shows how to publish to Info Exchange, how to republish an edited folder to Info Exchange, how both internal and external project team members can then view the files and upload more files to the folder once it is on Info Exchange, and how internal team members can receive the uploaded files in Project Center, unzip them, and republish them to the same folder to update them on Info Exchange.

This process has been divided into the following five sections:

  • To publish a project folder to Info Exchange

  • To update the project folder to Info Exchange because it has changed

  • To manage the published folder on Info Exchange and upload to it

  • To remove a shared folder from Info Exchange

Important: This procedure uses a folder from the Project Files activity center for the example. If you are publishing a document set (instead of a project folder) to Info Exchange, the workflow is basically the same as in the following procedures, except you would initiate it from the Project Document Sets activity center instead of the Project Files activity center.

If you are publishing a document set, be aware that only the selected document set is published. Any sub-document sets within the selected document set are not published.

To publish a project folder to Info Exchange

1.     Open a project in Project Center. If you are not already there, open the Project Files activity center by clicking Project Files from the Project Home activity center or from the Activities list.

2.     Select the project folder you want to publish, then click Info Exchange > Create Shared Folder from the Folder Tasks panel to open the Create Shared Folder dialog box.

3.     For this example, a folder called CM - Contract Management was selected above, and it is being renamed Newforma Mill - Plans for publishing, as shown below. Fill in the fields as necessary. Enter any comments in the Remarks tab. Click the Publish Options tab:

4.     You can choose to publish all of the files in the folder, or selected files from the folder. In this example, you would select  All Files in the Selected Folder from the Files to Publish drop-down list. A record copy .ZIP file can be saved to the location indicated in the Record Copy Folder field. You can save and log it in the Record Copies activity center by marking the Save a Record Copy of the Published Files checkbox (unless record copies were disabled for this project).

●        Select the External References option to use.

●        Mark the Notify Each Recipient checkbox to send an email message about the transfer to each recipient.

5.     Click the Upload Options tab:

●        Make sure the Allow Info Exchange Users to Upload Files checkbox is marked if you want external team members to be able to upload to and update the files in the folder.

●        Mark the Allow Access to Files Uploaded By Other Companies Immediately checkbox to allow all recipients (including CC members) of the shared folder to be recipients on subsequent uploads to the folder from both internal and external project team members. Each recipient will receive a notification that an upload has been made and will have immediate access to the upload on Info Exchange. If cleared, then files uploaded to Info Exchange will not be visible to anyone except the internal Project Center publisher of the shared folder. The internal publisher will then have to receive the uploaded files, extract them to the project folder, and then republish. At that time external users would be notified that new files are available. Choose one of the following options:

    • Choose Allow Access to Uploaded Files but do not Synchronize with Published Shared Folder to allow the user who is uploading files to include all recipients on the uploaded transfer so that they are notified that files are being uploaded and can access them through the uploaded file transfer. The files, however, will not be integrated into the shared folder until the internal Project Center sender receives them, extracts them to the project folder, and republishes them to Info Exchange.

    • Choose Automatically Synchronize Uploaded Files into Published Shared Folder to make files uploaded to the Info Exchange website immediately available in the published folder on Info Exchange. The internal Project Center user will still need to receive them and extract them to the published folder (unless the option below is checked), but other external users will have immediate access to them.

●        Mark the Automatically Synchronize Files Uploaded Via Info Exchange into the Associated Project Folder checkbox to have the Project Center Server automatically extract files that are uploaded to Info Exchange to the project folder after they are received.

This checkbox is only available if the Automatically Download Incoming Transfers option is selected in the Info Exchange tab of the Edit Project Settings dialog box.

Both the Automatically Synchronize Uploaded Files into Published Shared Folder option and the Automatically Synchronize Files Uploaded Via Info Exchange into the Associated Project Folder option must be selected to allow Info Exchange users to create and rename subfolders.

6.     Click the Synchronization Schedule tab:

●        Use this tab to schedule the publishing of shared folders. Click the New Time drop-down arrow to select from preset synchronization task times, or click New Time to open the Create Scheduled Task dialog box to schedule a new time (single or recurring) to synchronize (update) a published shared folder.

●        Enter your Windows Username and Password if required.

7.     Click OK when finished to open the Transfer to Info Exchange Options dialog box to edit the settings for the file transfer, including who can access it and reminder settings. Click OK to publish the contents to your Newforma Info Exchange server. The file transfer is logged in the All Outgoing category of the Info Exchange activity center.


If you select the Hide Recipient List option under Notification Options, only the internal member that created the shared folder is notified of changes to the folder. Additional notification recipients can be selected. If the option is disabled for a shared folder, everyone on the folder distribution list receives notifications.

8.     When you return to the Project Files activity center, the icon of the project folder changes to indicate that the folder was published, and the shared folder becomes a related item and is added to the Related Items tab, as shown here. The folder is now published to Info Exchange, and can be updated at any time via Project Center or the web.

You can change the list of recipients at anytime by selecting the published folder in the Related Items tab, then clicking Shared Folder > Add or Remove Recipients from the Tasks panel, which opens the Modify File Transfer Recipients dialog box.

9.     Continue with the next procedure if you want to continue the process.


To update the project folder to Info Exchange because it has changed

1.     Let's say that the files in the project folder have changed (files have been added or removed or the published folder was removed from Info Exchange). If you want to update the contents of the folder from Project Center, select the same folder in the Project Files activity center (in this example the Comparison folder), and click Synchronize Contents from the Tasks panel. The Transfer to Info Exchange Options dialog box opens. Edit the settings for the file transfer, including who can access it and reminder settings. Click OK to re-publish the contents to your Newforma Info Exchange Server.

2.     Optional: If you need to change any of the publishing options, select the folder and click Modify Shared Folder from the Tasks panel to open the Modify Shared Folder dialog box. Fill in the fields as necessary. Make sure the Allow Info Exchange Users to Upload Files checkbox is marked if you want external project team members to be able to upload and update the files in the folder.

In the Next Action field, choose one of the following:

  • Choose Synchronize Contents to republish the contents. This option opens the Transfer to Info Exchange Options dialog box (after you click OK) so you can edit the settings for the file transfer, including who can access it and reminder settings, and republish the contents to your Newforma Info Exchange server. The file transfer is logged in the All Outgoing category of the Info Exchange activity center.

  • Choose Notify New Recipients to add the new recipients to the transfer and send an email message to them that the transfer is available, without republishing the files. They will then be given the option to view the transfer, download the files, or go the Info Exchange website.

Click OK when finished.

3.     If the shared folder Files to Synchronize option on the Publish Options tab is set to Choose Specific Files, the Summary of Included Files and References dialog box opens. Mark the checkboxes of the files you want to republish to Info Exchange (files in red will be removed if they are checked). Click Continue to republish the contents to the folder on Info Exchange. Internal and external project team members can now view, manage, and upload files to the folder on Info Exchange.

4.     Continue with the next procedure if you want to continue the process.


To manage the published folder on Info Exchange and upload to it

The following steps can be performed by either an internal or external project team member on Info Exchange.

1.     Open a web browser and log onto Info Exchange.

2.     Click the project you want to open from the list of Projects.

3.     Click View > Files and Documents > Shared  Folders to view the list of shared folders for the project in the Shared Folders log. Click the name of the published folder in the Shared Folders panel (which is Newforma Mill - Plans in this example). The Folder Contents panel displays a list of all the files and subfolders contained in the shared folder, as shown in the following example:

4.     To upload files to the folder via Info Exchange, click the Tasks drop-down for the folder in the Shared Folders panel, the select Upload Files to open the Upload Files dialog box, shown here:

Depending on your browser, you may also be able to drag and drop files directly onto the desired folder or subfolder in the Folder Contents panel of the Shared Folders log. For more information, please refer to Drag and Drop Files to a Shared Folder.

5.     Select the folder or subfolder to which you want to upload files from Folder tree, then add the files you want to upload in the Files section of the dialog box.

6.     Click Upload to upload the files to the Newforma Mill - Plans folder on Info Exchange. In this example, the new file is added to the folder. The folder is updated to include the new file, and none of the other files are modified.

Depending on the project and shared folder settings, the uploaded files may be immediately available to other users. If this is not the case, an internal Project Center user must acknowledge receipt of the file from Info Exchange using Project Center before it can be seen by other users. Continue with the next procedure if you want to continue the process.

Newforma to Newforma (N2N) Setup Quick Reference Guide

This guide provides a reference for connecting a Newforma Project Center Project from your company to a project at another company that uses Project Center.

Click here to download a PDF of the reference guide.

Purpose

Newforma to Newforma (N2N) enables your company to seamlessly connect to other companies that use Project Center to streamline the coordination and exchange of critical project information. N2N uses a direct, secure communications channel between Project Center Servers and Info Exchange Servers within each company's corporate firewall.

Audience

Project Center administrators at the partnering companies.

Tasks covered

●        Connect two companies via N2N

●        Connect company projects

Notes

●        The Project Center administrators from each company should perform the following procedures on the phone.

●        Before connecting with Newforma to Newforma, partnering companies should enter into a trusted business relationship providing for the level of transparency required of the project information being shared.

●        You must know the URL of the Info Exchange Server of the company you are connecting to.

 

To connect two companies via N2N

It takes two consenting companies to complete an N2N connection. This section describes the steps required for a company (Company A) to initiate the connection and the corresponding steps that the other company (Company B) must take to confirm the connection.

1.     Before initiating a connection, the administrator at Company A needs to know the URL of Company B’s Info Exchange Server and the email address of the Project Center administrator at Company B.

2.     The company initiating the connection (Company A) must open the Project Center Administration activity center by clicking Project Center Administration from the Tasks panel of the My Project Center activity center, or from the Activities list.

3.      Click the Companies tab, then select the name of the company you want to connect to.

If you first need to add the company to Project Center, refer to the Add Company dialog box topic.

4.     Click Newforma to Newforma > Send Connection Request from the Tasks panel to open the Send Connection Request dialog box:



5.      Enter the URL of Company B's Info Exchange Server in the  Info Exchange Server Address field, as shown above. Click Verify to confirm the connection, then click OK. This generates an email message containing a link that the recipient at Company B will use to verify the connection.

You can get the URL from the link embedded in an Info Exchange email notification from the company you are connecting to.

6.     When the email message opens, enter the email address of the contact who will be confirming the connection request at Company B and click Send.

7.     Company B: The recipient of the connection request must open the email message and click Link My Company to complete the connection request, as shown here:


No email message is returned to the contact at Company A who initiated the request.

8.      In the following dialog box, the recipient must click Open in Newforma Project Center.


9.     Company B: When the Confirm Integration Request dialog box opens (as shown below), the contact at Company B who is responding must verify that the company name in the Matching Company field is correct, then click OK.

If Company A is not automatically selected in the Matching Company field, the recipient at Company B needs to click Browse to locate and select Company A.


A confirmation message similar to the following appears when the connection is complete:


10.  The connection appears as Connected in the Connection Status column of the Project Center Administration activity center Companies tab at both companies, as shown here:


 

To connect company projects

This procedure can be done at either of the connected companies. The two companies must be connected before performing this procedure, as described in the procedure above.

Both of the projects must be available on Info Exchange.

1.     Initiating company: If you are not already there, open the Project Center Administration activity center by clicking Project Center Administration from the Tasks panel of the My Project Center activity center, or from the Activities list.

2.     Click the Projects tab.

3.     Select the project you want to connect to another company's project.

4.     Click Newforma to Newforma> Connect with Another Company's Project from the Tasks panel to open the Select Connected Company dialog box:


5.     Select the company whose project you want to connect to and click OK. The following confirmation message opens, which contains information about the connection. Click Yes to continue.


6.     Open the email message (as shown below) and enter the email address of the contact who will be confirming the connection at the company receiving the connection request and click Send.

7.     Recipient company: The company receiving the connection request must open the email message and click Select a Matching Project and Complete the Connection to select the project to connect to and complete the connection, as shown here:


8.     In the following dialog box, click Open in Newforma Project Center:


9.     When the Confirm Project Connect Request dialog box opens (as shown here), the recipient company must click Browse next to the Associated Project field to open the Select a Project dialog box to locate and select the corresponding project. Click OK when finished.


Mark the Reply to Sender with a Confirmation Email checkbox to send an email message to the contact who initiated the request.

The following confirmation message appears when the project connection is complete. Click OK.


 

The email message sent to the initiator will be similar to the following:


10.  The projects are now connected and the connected company's name is listed in the Connected To column at both companies, as shown here:

Adding new office location

​​​​​​​Under Navigation 

  1. Select Configuration.
  2. User Groups.
  3. Select Card Administrator and Edit.
  1. Select Permissions tab
  2. Select Cardholder Fields
  3. Double click to edit Location 
  4. Enter new office in List Items field.  You will need to use up down arrow keys to scroll up and down.
  5. Hit OK to save and OK again.  

Close Access It! Program for setting to take place, then open program again.


Creating and assigning new Access Levels 

Under Navigation select Configuration then Access Levels and click New in top left corner.

Create New Access Level.

  1. Enter the Access Level Name in the top field. 
  2. Select the drop down for Timezone and select the appropriate Timezone.
  3. Scroll down and select the location / readers.
  4. Click right arrow.
  5. Confirmed the assigned readers are correct.
  6. Click save at the top.

Assign Access Level to a cardholder.

  1. Under Navigation select Main then Cardholders from left hand side.
  2. Enter the name and search for cardholder.
  3. Double click the card number to edit card.
  4. Select Access Levels tab.
  5. Under Access Levels – Available, select the appropriate Access Level
  6. Click the right arrow.
  7. Confirm appropriate Access Levels are correct under Assigned.
  8. Click Save to apply Access Levels to that card.


Important note:  

Hardware / SCP / Readers names must not be changed as they are linked directly to reporting that is name sensitive for each office location.  If a change is needed, please inform IT.

IT Closet or Server Room Door access must be approved by IT for any Access Level assignment.

Add a Conference Room to a Teams Meeting


Join A Teams Meeting with Room Audio:

Start Teams Meeting on laptop, however, choose Room Audio.  Type name of the conference room, for Nashville type CR Nash.  All Teams Room Systems in Nashville will be shown.  Select the room you are in and click Join




Add a Teams Conference Room to an ongoing Teams Meeting:

Select participants in top of Teams Meetings controls.  Type the name of the Conference Room and select Request to Join.  Conference Rooms are just like participants and can be added to meetings.


On the Conference Room Touch Panel click Accept


If you are attending a Teams Meeting in a conference room, always make sure that you join your laptop with Don’t use audio.  This will prevent echo or reverb with the Conference Room System

Use the steps below to configure Password-less login for the Microsoft Authenticator app. *This will allow you to login to Microsoft apps without entering your password, but keep in mind you will still have to enter your password to login to your computer. 

1. Set up the Microsoft Authenticator app if you have not already. Instructions for this can be found here: How to Set up the Authenticator app

2. In the Authenticator app, select your Gresham Smith account:



3. Click the 'Set up phone sign-in' button:



4. Click 'Continue':



5. Click 'Finish':



6. The next time you are prompted to login to a Microsoft app, enter your email and click 'Next':



7. You will see a number displayed on your screen. Open the Authenticator app on your phone.



8. Enter the number in the Authenticator app and click 'yes'. You will now be logged in without having to enter your password.

✓ Backup Policy for Gresham Smith (ServiceNow Link)

Description: File Servers File data from all sites is replicated in near real-time to servers in Azure for backup and site recovery. This replication only maintains the current state of the data. A virtual Machine level backup of the VM is done once a day using …

ID: 9e45ade3-46be-460b-9ba6-8b2b8771356d

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Backup-Policy-for-Gresham,-Smith-and-Partners.aspx

https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/microsoft-onedrive-blog/new-updates-to-onedrive-and-sharepoint-team-site-versioning/ba-p/204390 https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-platform-service-description/service-health-and-continuity https://wwwimages2.adobe.com/content/dam/acom/en/security/pdfs/CCE_security_whitepaper.pdf

File Servers

File data from all sites is replicated in near real-time to servers in Azure for backup and site recovery. This replication only maintains the current state of the data. 
A virtual Machine level backup of the VM is done once a day using Azure VM backup into online storage. The backup is done overnight around midnight. The backups can either be mounted to another server for file recovery or the entire server can be recovered.​
Daily backups are kept for 30 days.
One backup a month is kept for 24 months.
One backup a quarter (January, April, July, October) is kept for 5 years.
The backup process generates email alerts on failed backups and appropriate steps are taken to resolve the issue.

File servers are configured with Volume Shadow copy that makes a virtual copy twice a day around 7am and 12pm. The users can access the previous versions and restore a file themselves in many cases. The retention is governed by the disk space available for the changed data and the change rate on the volume. The goal is to have 1 week of snapshots available.

A DFS name space is maintained for each volume. All user access should be through the name space. Both the local copy and the remote copy are included in the name space so the file access can be redirected to the secondary copy either automatically when the primary is unavailable or in some cases it is administratively controlled to make sure that everyone is working on the primary copy.

Databases

Database data is backed up to file backups and the accounting (Vantagepoint) and HR databases are also backed up using a backup agent. The backups are stored in the Azure storage above and subject to the same retention.

Once a year after closing the previous year a financial back is made at retained for 7 years.

Email

Email data is stored in Office 365 and managed by Microsoft. By Risk Management policy no backup of email is kept for over 30 days.
Deleted email goes into the Deleted Items folder and is kept for 30 days.
When they are removed from the Deleted Items folder, they go into the Recoverable Items Folder. Items in the Recoverable Items Folder are maintained for 14 days.
People can recover deleted items from either of these locations without admin assistance.​
 

Teams and OneDrive
 


Teams document libraries and OneDrive data have versioning enabled by Microsoft with a minimum of 100 major versions retained. It is not possible to disable versioning or set it to less than 100 versions.

https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/microsoft-onedrive-blog/new-updates-to-onedrive-and-sharepoint-team-site-versioning/ba-p/204390

SharePoint

SharePoint document libraries have versioning enabled with a minimum of 100 versions retained.

In SharePoint, items are retained for 93 days from the time you delete them from their original location. They stay in the site Recycle Bin the entire time, unless someone deletes them from there or empties that Recycle Bin. In that case, the items go to the site collection Recycle Bin, where they stay for the remainder of the 93 days.



Office 365 data reliability policy from: https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-platform-service-description/service-health-and-continuity

Microsoft ensures that customer data is available whenever it is needed through the following features:

Data storage and redundancy: Customer data is stored in a redundant environment with robust data protection capabilities to enable availability, business continuity, and rapid recovery. Multiple levels of data redundancy are implemented, ranging from redundant disks to guard against local disk failure to continuous, full data replication to a geographically diverse data center.

Data monitoring: Microsoft services maintain high levels of performance by:

Monitoring databases:
​
Blocked processes
Packet loss
Queued processes
Query latency

Completing preventative maintenance: Preventative maintenance includes database consistency checks, periodic data compression, and error log reviews.​

Autodesk BIM360 data

Daily publish – A script that runs daily and publishes all of the models on BIM360. Published models are in BIM360 but essentially a different storage location from the live model. (This is or daily backup)
Versions in BIM360 each time users’ sync
These synced versions are per user and date stamped
The synced versions can only be accessed from within the Revit interface but are stored in the cloud
Local downloaded copies from 
A copy of the live model is downloaded when a user opens the file, so they are basically working locally. They sync the model to push changes to the cloud. These local copies are stored on the user's machine, and we can access those as an additional backup if the above options do not work
The only time data can be lost is If a user does not save locally when a sync fails

Adobe Creative Cloud

User generated content is redundantly stored in multiple data centers within a region and on multiple devices in each data center. Stored content is synchronously and automatically replicated to other data center facilities within the region so that data integrity is maintained even in the event of data loss in two locations.
https://wwwimages2.adobe.com/content/dam/acom/en/security/pdfs/CCE_security_whitepaper.pdf


Adobe Document Cloud

https://acrobat.adobe.com/content/dam/doc-cloud/en/pdfs/Document-Cloud-Security-Overview.pdf​​​​​​​​

✓ Computer Update and Downtime Policy (ServiceNow Link)

Description: work in progress do not approve Operating System Updates IMPORTANT: To keep our systems patched, we encourage everyone to install security updates as soon as possible. Preferably the day they are released. Not only will this help protect our compute…

ID: cbfc11c4-cf5b-4bbb-b62c-661ac0561eb7

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Computer-Update-and-Downtime-Policy.aspx

/Pages/PortalHome.aspx

work in progress do not approve


Operating System Updates

IMPORTANT: To keep our systems patched, we encourage everyone to install security updates as soon as possible. Preferably the day they are released. Not only will this help protect our computers from threats, it will help you avoid an awkward update install and reboot if you wait until the deadline. 


Windows 10 Security and Feature Updates

Windows 10 receives two types of updates. Security Updates and Feature Updates.

  1. Security Updates: To reduce risk, these updates will be installed the 2nd Tuesday of each month as they are released from Microsoft.
  2. Feature Updates: Windows 10 has transitioned to a continuous update model. Under this model Microsoft will release feature updates on a regular basis. These updates will go to consumers first. Then about 4 months later they will be released to businesses. The delay allows bugs to be worked out before the business release. When we receive these updates we will further divide it into a two-tiered approach:
    • Tier 1: About 4 months after the consumer release we will release these updates to our early adopter group. We target about 15% of our Windows 10 users in this group.
    • Tier 2:  The rest of our Windows 10 users will receive Feature and Quality updates about 30 days after Tier 1.

For installation instructions see here 


Windows 7 Security Updates

Microsoft releases Windows 7 updates the second Tuesday of each month. Installing these updates soon after the release is important to keep our computers secure. When you receive notification of an update, please install it at your earliest convenience. (If you wait until the deadline it may not be convenient.)

We will be releasing Windows 7 updates in two Tiers:

  • Tier 1:  Receive Windows 7 Updates 2 weeks after Microsoft releases them.  Will have 14 days to install at their time of choosing.  After 14 days, the updates will install and your computer will reboot. 15% of Windows 7 users.
  • Tier 2: Receive Windows 7 updates 6 days after Tier 1.  Will have 21 days to install at their time of choosing.  After 21 days, the updates will install and your computer will reboot. 

For installation instructions see here


Software Updates 

IMPORTANT: We recommend you install any applications you are notified  of via Software Center ahead of the Monday Morning maintenance window to avoid interruptions in your workflow.  If you happen to be working during this window, we recommend you save often as you will likely not be notified before the system restarts.


SCCM Maintenance Window

Every Monday Morning between 1am&4am, Microsoft System Center Configuration Manager will enter maintenance mode.  If your computer is powered on, it will install any pending applications that have been released from IT.  During this time frame, the computer will restart if an installation requires a restart. 


Check for Software Updates or Install Software Updates as notified

To install applications via Software Center follow these steps:

  1. Go to Start
  2. Type 'Software Center' in the search bar
  3. Click on Software Center
  4. Once inside, choose the application you want and click it to highlight it.
  5. Hit the blue INSTALL button at the bottom right corner
  6. The installation will take about 20 minutes.

For installation instructions see here 


Microsoft Office Updates

  1. With Outlook open click File
  2. Left hand side select Office Account
  3. Middle screen click Update Options button beside Office Updates
  4. Click Update Now
  5. May be prompted to close Office Programs, Skype for Business or Internet Explorer


NOTE: Be sure to save any active documents before starting the download. You will not be able to use any Office products while the download and installation is running.

For installation instructions see here 


Monthly System Downtime

The Third Thursday of every month between 6pm Thursday and 6am Friday CST is GS&P Monthly System Downtime.  During this time some resources may be unavailable.  Be sure to check the Bug email or and http://gspportal/Pages/PortalHome.aspx website on this day for more information on what resources will be unavailable.   We use this time to patch servers, network resources, move resources and to update software.

✓ Converting Microsoft Word file to PDF for SharePoint and Content Search (ServiceNow Link)

Dimensions: 1075x847

SOLUTION: branding fonts must be embedded in the individual MS Word file and, using the GSP​​​​​​​_PDF Creator 3 option, printed to PDF to render a completely searchable file.


Embed the Fonts

  1. In MS Word, open the file you would like to convert
  2. Click File, Options (bottom, left)​​​​​​​

      3. From the pop-up options menu, click Save



  1. On the bottom-right of the save options window, find the Preserve Fidelity when sharing this document section
  2. Make sure that the current document is selected in the drop-down
  3. Select the options:
    1. Embed fonts in this file and the option, and
    2. ​Embed only the characters used in the document​

  1. Click OK
  2. ​​Save your updated word document

The fonts are now embedded in the working document.​



Converting to PDF

  1. To convert the MS Word document, press Ctrl + P or File, Print
  2. From the print menu, choose the GSP_PDF Creator 3 as the printer
  1. Click Print
  2. Confirmation may take a few seconds to show
  3. When the GSP_PDF Creator 3 pop-up is shown, click to the right of the File Name box to choose the save location
  4. Optionally, you can click the checkbox "Open destination folder after creation" to open the file explorer save location
  1. Click Save
  2. After a few seconds, Adobe Acrobat will open with the newly converted file
  3. To ensure the fonts were embedded, click File, Properties (or Ctrl + D)
  4. When the documents properties window pop-up opens, click the Fonts tab
  1. Scroll through the list to find the Gresham Smith branding fonts (Noe Display and Atlas Grotesk)
    • If the fonts cannot be found, the process failed
    • Please contact the helpdesk for further assistance
  2. ​Upon successful completion, you are now ready to close the file and upload to SharePoint​

ID: 0795f30a-08ab-4e3f-84f1-44f2d6be28fe

Dimensions: 1933x787

Image ID: 60cfb8ec-123c-4bef-853a-8b2f9197939c

Path: images/0795f30a-08ab-4e3f-84f1-44f2d6be28fe/d6000_3.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=51b125482bc1ae105be0ff10de91bffd

Dimensions: 779x329


This document provides an overview of the D6000 docking station and best practices when using one. The D6000 docking station can be found at most desks firm-wide. 

1. There are two ways you can connect to the D6000 docking station. If your computer has the smaller USB-C port, this is the preferred way to connect. 
2. If your computer does not have the smaller USB-C connection, use the larger USB-A connection. The smaller USB-C connector will plug into the back of the USB-A connector.

 3. If one or both of your displays are not working, try these steps in order:
  • disconnect your laptop from the docking station
  • remove the power cord from the back of the docking station for 15 seconds
  • reconnect the power cord to the docking station
  • reconnect your laptop to the docking station
  • after a few seconds your displays should now be fixed

4. Always be sure to connect a power cord to your laptop when using the docking station. Although the docking station provides some power through a USB-C connection, it is not enough to fully power and charge your laptop. Connect a power cord to your laptop to ensure you're running at full speed.

Follow the steps below to enable the auto-reply for Outlook via a web browser.


 

1. Open a browser, log into https://outlook.office365.com with your Gresham Smith credentials. Then, click on the gear icon for Settings, and scroll down and click 'View all Outlook settings'.
 



2. Under Mail -> Automatic Replies toggle Automatic Replies to on. Now you can set a date range and type your 
   message. Click Save at the top to activate your message.


 

** NOTE** If you send replies outside of Gresham Smith, please also check the box to send to contacts only. This will prevent confirming a good email address to a spammer while you're out of the office.

✓ Gresham Smith Always On VPN (ServiceNow Link)

Description: The Gresham Smith laptop is pre-configured for accessing the Gresham Smith VPN network when working outside the office. When working from home or from a remote location verify that the laptop is connected either through a wi-fi signal or wired netwo…

ID: 3d59452d-c305-4d7d-b494-1a62d7ac17f9

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Always-On-VPN.aspx

Image ID: 13a7b08c-b8d8-4222-828b-cfa80f642bde

Path: images/3d59452d-c305-4d7d-b494-1a62d7ac17f9/1692802962841Untitled.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=0291a1482bc1ae105be0ff10de91bfa7

Dimensions: 364.9941762873051x627.9899800230893

The Gresham Smith laptop is pre-configured for accessing the Gresham Smith VPN network when working outside the office. When working from home or from a remote location verify that the laptop is connected either through a wi-fi signal or wired network cable. 

NOTE: When working in Autodesk products or on CADD drawings, a wired network cable is the preferred method. 

The Gresham Smith Always On VPN should connect automatically in the background allowing access to Gresham Smith resources such as network files and folders, and applications. 

If you have problems accessing network resources and/or applications, click the wireless/network icon in the bottom right corner of the laptop's screen, verify that the Gresham Smith Always On VPN displays "connected' for one of the listings. 

If connected is not displayed, select one of the displayed Gresham Smith Always On VPN listings and if requested input your login information. Once connected, access to the Gresham network resources should now be available.

​​​

If the Gresham Smith Always On VPN continues experiencing issues, RESTART the laptop.

If problems continue, reach out to the IT Help Desk at helpdesk@greshamsmith.com.

When scanning from the office copiers you have the option to choose either "Scan to Email" or "Scan to Folder". Scan to Email works well for smaller scan jobs, typically under 20MB in size. Scan to Folder is the better option for larger scan jobs and can be accomplished using the steps below. 


1. Start by scanning your badge at the copier to login. If you haven't already registered your badge click this link to see how. How to Register Your Badge at a Copier



 2. Choose the 'Scan' option




 3. Choose the 'Scan to Folder' option and follow the instructions on the printer to complete the scan.


4. Locate your scans in the appropriate network folder. For example, Nashville scans will go to \\global.gsp\data\usr_data\na_usr_data\Temp\SCANS\Papercut, and other scans will go to \\global.gsp\data\scans depending on office location. 

     ** Once you have received the scans you NEED to then move them to your project folder as needed. 

NOTE: The documents will be left in the folder for up to three days before they are purged from the folder.

✓ GS Custom Tools Installation (ServiceNow Link)

Description: Install Instructions: Using the Installer: To install the GreshamSmith toolbar the user needs to have pyRevit installed already. (Latest version of pyRevit can be found at https://github.com/eirannejad/pyRevit/releases ). Once pyRevit has been insta…

ID: d4515a24-2eaa-4bee-9a0f-538036824c1f

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/GS-Custom-Tools-Installation.aspx

Image ID: c6957ce7-c6a6-4499-afd8-1178379e033b

Path: images/d4515a24-2eaa-4bee-9a0f-538036824c1f/GSCustom1.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=6b81a1482bc1ae105be0ff10de91bf21

Dimensions: 1184x665.26

https://github.com/eirannejad/pyRevit/releases file://///global.gsp/data/gspm/CAD_ADSK_STDS/Revit/GsTools%20and%20run%20the%20application file://///global.gsp/data/gspm/CAD_ADSK_STDS/Revit/GsTools file://///global.gsp/data/nf/na_nf01/19631.00_010/_PT/development/revit/GreshamSmith file://///global.gsp/data/gspm/CAD_ADSK_STDS/Revit/Dynamo

Install Instructions:
 

Using the Installer:
 

 
 

To install the GreshamSmith toolbar the user needs to have pyRevit installed already. (Latest version of pyRevit can be found at https://github.com/eirannejad/pyRevit/releases).

Once pyRevit has been installed, copy the shortcut of GS Custom Tools.exe at \\global.gsp\data\gspm\CAD_ADSK_STDS\Revit\GsToolsRevit\GsTools and run the application.  Once the application has been opened the UI pops up and the user can choose the set of custom tools they need.

NOTE : Once the radio button is selected it automatically creates the required config file in the user's Appdata - pyRevit folder.

NOTES: 
 

The GreshamSmith Toolbar is a pyRevit extension which is stored in: \\global.gsp\data\gspm\CAD_ADSK_STDS\Revit\GsTools

 The toolbar can be installed using the exe file called "GS Custom Tools". (This replaces your pyRevit config file)

(PT ONLY test tools:  \\global.gsp\data\nf\na_nf01\19631.00_010\_PT\development\revit\GreshamSmith Custom Tools Extension). The location of this extension in the server may cause certain delays (slower than pyRevit tools) since Revit has to get the information from the drive to execute it each time whereas the pyRevit tools are on the local.
 

The reason the tools are on the server is that, more tools can be added to the folder, and it will automatically update in every user's toolbar when they reload pyRevit or restart Revit.
 

Some of the tools might be Dynamo graphs that require packages to be installed on the user's local Dynamo folder. These packages can be installed using a PowerShell script (called DynamoPackages.ps2 at \\global.gsp\data\gspm\CAD_ADSK_STDS\Revit\Dynamo) that has been written but in order for it to work the user needs to open that version of dynamo at least once (So that a folder is created for that specific version in program data where the packages need to reside).
 

If users decide to install the toolbar using the second method, then they MUST install the General tools in addition to the others. (Since the general toolbar contains the hooks that extract Revit data for The Analytics dashboard).
 

Users might also need to install dynamo version 2.0.2 or higher if they are using Revit 2019 and lower and do not already have the Dynamo 2.0.X versions.

*** If you plan to use the Teams Room System when scheduling a Teams Meeting, be sure to invite the room when you're scheduling through Outlook. If you invite the room properly, you will see a Join Meeting Button on the Teams Room System display a few minutes before your meeting start time. This is the preferred way to schedule a Teams Meeting in a Conference Room. However, if you are in an impromptu Teams meeting and need to add a Teams Room System to the call, follow the steps below. If you plan to connect both your laptop and a Teams Room System to a Teams Meeting, be sure to join your laptop to the meeting with "no audio" to avoid an echo. ***

1. In your Teams meeting, click the 'Participants' button




2. In the Participants search box, search for the Conference Room you are in.



3. Select the Conference Room you would like to add to the meeting and click the 'Request to Join' button.



4. The Teams Room System will ring. Click the 'Join' button on the Teams Room System display. ** If your computer is connected to the meeting with audio, be sure to mute YOUR microphone in the Teams meeting and mute YOUR speaker to avoid an echo from the Teams Room System. **



5. The Teams Room System will now join the meeting.

You can add a Teams Channel's calendar to your Outlook following the steps below.


  1. From the appropriate Channel, click the Calendar tab
  2. Click the carrot next to Calendar and select 'Go to website'. This will open a new browser page.
  3. Click the Calendar menu tab, then click 'Connect to Outlook'
  4. Accept the prompts to connect to Outlook
  5. In Outlook, switch to the Calendar view by clicking the calendar icon
  6. You should see the calendar listed under 'Other Calendars'
  7. ** Optional ** You can rename the calendar by right-clicking on the name. You can also drag it to a different place on your list of calendars.

✓ How to Create a Team in Microsoft Teams (ServiceNow Link)

Description: Ad-Hoc Teams: Employees can create "Ad-Hoc Teams" without consulting the I.T. Department. These ad-hoc teams allow you to send messages and share files with your colleagues. Instructions for this can be found here: How to Create an Ad-Hoc Team using…

ID: d8294936-2069-4b29-a72b-d1137ae828a5

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/How-to-Create-a-Team-in-Microsoft-Teams.aspx

https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/How-to-create-an-ad-hoc-Team-using-Teams-Chat-Group.aspx https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Help-Desk.aspx https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Help-Desk.aspx https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Help-Desk.aspx
  • Ad-Hoc Teams: Employees can create "Ad-Hoc Teams" without consulting the I.T. Department. These ad-hoc teams allow you to send messages and share files with your colleagues. Instructions for this can be found here: How to Create an Ad-Hoc Team using Teams Chat Group
  • Teams Channels: Every Market and Corporate Services department has a Team. So, all employees should be in one of those Teams. If you have a topic that is not already covered in your Market or Department Team, use the General channel to post. If you think a separate channel is needed, coordinate that with your MVP (Market Vice President) or department head.
  • Project Teams - Internal Employees Only: If you need a Team created for a specific project, and only Gresham Smith employees will be included, please submit a Help Desk ticket here. Include information including what the Team should be named, the channels that should be included, and who should be the Team admins. These internal project Team requests will be considered on a case-by-case basis. The Director of Project Delivery Excellence will be notified of the request such that a conversation regarding documentation protocol will occur with the project PM.

  • Project Teams - Internal & External Employees: If you need a Team created that will include non-Gresham Smith employees, please contact the Director of Project Delivery Excellence to begin the conversation.

  • New Teams - Exception Required: If you believe you have a need for a new Team that does not fall into one of the categories above, then submit the request to the Help Desk. We will work with you and the appropriate approvers to evaluate and configure any new Teams.

You can enable an out-of-office reply from the Outlook app on your Android phone. Follow the steps below to use this feature. 
 


** NOTE - you will not be able to set a date range (beginning and end date) through the Outlook app. **
 


1. Open your Outlook app and tap your profile picture.
 


 



2. Tap the Settings gear icon in the lower-left corner.
 



 



3. Tap your Gresham Smith account.
 



 



4. Tap 'Automatic replies'
 



 



5. Toggle the 'Automatic replies' button on and start typing your message.
 



 



6. Tap the check icon in the top-right to save and activate your message. When you want to turn it off, return here and toggle it off.

You can start an impromptu call/meeting from a Teams Room System in the office. 

1. From the Teams Room System click the 'New Meeting' button.


2. In the Search bar that says 'find someone or dial a number' search for an employee and select their profile picture.


3. Click the 'Invite' button to call the employee.


4. The employee will receive a Teams call. They will need to accept the call to join the meeting. 


5. You will now be connected to the meeting with the employee you just called.

2. After the app installs, click the 'Open' button.

✓ How to move a PST to the Outlook Online Archive (ServiceNow Link)

Description: Many people have created Outlook Data Files and Outlook Archives also known as .pst files.  These are files that contain emails and other items from Outlook.  .PST files have been a convenient way to keep email overflow but they have been problemati…

ID: de6676f6-9d15-4fc4-b71c-815ce514afba

URL: https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/How-to-move-a-PST-to-the-Outlook-Online-Archive.aspx

Dimensions: 201x111

Image ID: 0fc7ad14-582c-4c20-9a5c-8e8a29dcb7e8

Path: images/de6676f6-9d15-4fc4-b71c-815ce514afba/3.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=fe8129cc3b0d2e108c68249693e45a91

Dimensions: 367x176

Image ID: 5dd4857f-925f-4b52-b0a8-6c0dd4c01bd1

Path: images/de6676f6-9d15-4fc4-b71c-815ce514afba/4.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=0f8129cc3b0d2e108c68249693e45a89

Dimensions: 263x622

Image ID: 8838966b-bf18-42b9-8d41-cd28f9925aaf

Path: images/de6676f6-9d15-4fc4-b71c-815ce514afba/5.png

ServiceNow URL: https://greshamsmith.service-now.com/sys_attachment.do?sys_id=438161482bc1ae105be0ff10de91bf88

Dimensions: 356x294

Many people have created Outlook Data Files and Outlook Archives also known as .pst files.  These are files that contain emails and other items from Outlook.  .PST files have been a convenient way to keep email overflow but they have been problematic and difficult to manage.  With Office 365 there is now a better way to manage and keep up with these emails. Move them to your online archive.  This article explains how to move messages out of your .pst file and into your Online Archive.

***PST files should NOT be stored in OneDrive - they will cause you to run out of space due to the way they are backed up***

Step 1: Locate your Outlook Data File (PST) file in Outlook
When you locate the PST file in Outlook, open the folders of the emails you are wanting to move to the new Online Archive. Hint: It is best to create your own unique folders in the Online Archive and then move emails accordingly.  




Step 2 : Choosing emails from PST folders to move to the Online Archive
After you have found the emails in the folders you are wanting to move, highlight the first email in the row 



After you select the first email, just go down about 100 email messages in the column and HOLD DOWN THE SHIFT KEY and then select the email.

This will highlight the group of emails.  We suggest moving small amounts of emails at a time to avoid delays.

Step 3: Move your emails to the Online Archive folder
Now that you have your row of emails selected, let's move them to the folder you created in the Online Archive mailbox. You are going to RIGHT CLICK  the emails you have chosen and select MOVE. From the list provided to the right you can choose the folder you created in Online Archive or if it isn't listed select OTHER FOLDER and it will pull up this dialogue box.

You can choose the Online Archive and the folder you created( I created the Last Months Emails folder as a demo)and then once you highlight the folder ,hit the OK button.  Your emails will move from the PST file to the Online Archive folder you created. Please give Outlook time to respond, depending on how many emails you are moving, this will take some time.



Step 4: Repeat Steps 1-3
Based on the amount of time it took to move that first batch of emails you can adjust the number of emails you select for future batches.  Just follow the above steps to continue moving emails from the PST to the Online Archive.

Tips and tricks:

 We highly recommend you don't move entire email folders because the size can get quite large and may take a very long time to move and may error out.

https://gspnet4.sharepoint.com/sites/Information-Technology/SitePages/Add-a-Conference-Room-to-a-Teams-Meeting.aspx

Does the conference room have a device under the TV that looks like this?   If so, Scroll Down to Neat Teams Room System Instructions, for additional controls.

How to use any Microsoft Teams Room Device.

Microsoft Teams Rooms can be used for Zoom, Cisco Webex, and Teams Meetings.  In order for the system to work correctly the Conference Room must be invited to the meeting.  The Conference Room is a participant in a meeting so it must be invited.

If you are joining the meeting with your laptop. Always choose to join the meeting, with “Don't use audio”.  If you have an echo in the room, most likely there is someone in the room that joined with computer audio.  That will cause an echo in the Conference Room.

Make sure Room Display is on the correct input.  The TV or Teams Room System should have a label for what input the TV should be set to.  If there are multiple TVs in the Conference Room, then the TV input should NOT be change.

If the Conference Room Touch Panel shows the meeting square with the Join button in bottom right, then the Room System can one click Join a meeting.  Examples shown with Green Arrows.

If the Conference Room was NOT invited to the meeting or the meeting invite was not formatted correctly.  The meeting will not have a Join Button as shown below.

You can still join the Conference Room into a Teams meeting manually. Click here for Instructions. This ONLY works for Teams Meetings, does NOT work for Zoom or Cisco Webex Meetings.

You can always join a meeting early; however, you may be placed into a waiting room if the external host has not​​​​​​​ started the meeting. 

Teams Meeting in progress.  Notice the Join button is available and highlighted. Teams Meeting logo is shown in upper right corner.


Some rooms the Join button is on the Left side.

Zoom Meeting in progress.  Notice the Join Button is available and highlighted. Zoom Meeting logo is shown in upper right corner.

Cisco Webex Meeting in progress. Notice the Join Button is available and highlighted. Cisco Webex logo is shown in upper right corner.

Making Direct Calls:

To dial an external number or call an employee or another conference room, click the call button.  Either type the person, or conference room you want to call, or use the dial pad to call an external number.  Click call to make the call.

Joining Meetings:

Click Join Button to Join the Conference Room into the meeting.  You may need to unmute the room microphones.  Please check the online doc for your particular meeting room.

Once the Conference Room has joined you can Invite others or change some of the Teams Settings.

The top right allows you add participants to the meeting.  The Bottom Bar you can change Content view for in room display, Sound volume, turn camera on or off, mute and hang up.

Show Screen Sharing Full Screen:

Teams Rooms now default to show chat and participants while screen sharing, which takes up some room.  To show the Screen Share full screen you can turn off Chat and Select Focus on Content.


Once chat is off select Focus on content.

​​​​​​​Participants settings:

To add Participants in the top right, enter the name and click Request to Join.

You can Mute, Spotlight, Pin and Remove Participants.

Content View for in Room displays:

To change how content is shown on the In Room Display press the button in yellow below.

You can change the Displays to only show Content, or Content and People, or People Only.  You are also able to change to show more participants with Large Gallery.

Hang Up or Leave a Meeting:

Don’t forget to hang up on the Touch Panel so the conference room leaves the meeting.

 

Neat Teams Room System Instructions:  

Room Camera Framing:  Want Room Camera view instead of Individual Frames? 

After Joining a meeting slide the bar to the left as shown below. Change room camera settings:  Auto Room Framing, Individual Framing, or Just Room View no Framing.

Recommended is Auto framing: Group. 

How to use HDMI or BYOD mode:

This requires the Conference Table to have two cables, an HDMI and a USB / USB-C cable.  Shown below.

HDMI mode for In Room Only Presentations:

Simply connect the HDMI Cable to your laptop.  The TV should now show your screen automatically.  If the conference room has two TV's, then only the left TV will be presented.  HDMI mode is useful for when vendors come in or when need to watch Gresham Smith Town Halls on YouTube.

 

BYOD Mode:

This requires both the HDMI Cable and USB / USB-C Cable to be connected to a laptop.  Once connected enable BYOD Mode.  Slide the bar to the left.

Select BYOD Mode: This allows the Neat Room device to work with Any Video Conferencing Applications.

If all cables are not connected the TV will show which cables still needs connected.  Show below is missing HDMI cable.

Once all cables are connected.  The TV will show your laptop screen, and you can choose Camera Layout.  Recommended is Auto framing: Group.

Setup Devices in your Teams Application:  

Inside Teams on the laptop that has both HDMI and USB / USB-C cable connected. Go to Settings by clicking the three dots next to profile picture in upper right corner of Teams Application and choose Settings.

Select Devices on left side in Settings.  Confirm or change Audio Settings for both Speaker and Microphone to show Echo Cancelling Speakerphone (Neat…).

Scroll down a bit more to Devices, Camera and change or confirm Neat Bar Camera is selected.  The preview should show the room.

Description
 

JOTools is a group of Revit Add-Ins tools that were developed by Juan Osborne. Through research, the Practice Technology team has found that these tools helps to increase productivity for our design team at Gresham Smith.   The Transfer Project Standards tool is a key software development as project templates hold virtually no company standards, therefore, these standards will be transferred from discipline's library files using the Transfer Project Standards JOTools.
 

JO Tools Transfer Single
 

Tired of all or nothing regular transfer standards? With Transfer Single you will be able to transfer just one item of most of the standards, event to multiple files at one time! Also you will be able to copy additional elements like views, printing setups, section boxes; worksets... even legends with contents!
 

Easily transfer project standards such as legends, schedules, and views from one project to many project files using the JO Tools TransferSingle function. 

Step 1: Prepare Files For Transfer
 

Ensure all files, source files and target files are open. Remember you can transfer to multiple files at the same time but all must be open.


 

Step 2: Start JOTools ->TransferSingle
 

In Revit, activate the JOTools tab, then select the Transfer Single icon. 
 


 

MassLoad Families

MassLoad fill find any rfa files under selected folder and subfolder and will show you as tree structure.
 

Step 1: Start JOTools ->MassLoad Families
 

In Revit, activate the JOTools tab, then select the MassLoad Families icon. 
 



 




 



MassSave Families

MassSave will save all listed families from project and will let you save it to a target folder. Select folder, check wanted families then press Save Families.
 

Step 1: Start JOTools ->MassSave Families

In Revit, activate the JOTools tab, then select the MassSave Families icon.

There are a couple of different ways to get an impromptu meeting ​started with just a few clicks. You can add audio, video and share your screen. 


FROM YOUR CALENDER

​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​Go to ​​Calendar on the left side of Teams, then select Meet now in the upper right hand corner.



In your video preview, give your meeting a title, choose whether you want to use video, and pick your preferred audio source. When you're ready, click the Join Now button. 



Your meeting is now running. To Invite people to your meeting:

Type and select the names of the team members you want to invite to the meeting. Those that answer will be immediately added to the meeting.



Just like with scheduled meetings, everyone who attends your meeting will continue to have access to the meeting chat and anything else people share in the meeting (like files and meeting notes), even after the meeting ends.

To rejoin the same meeting anytime, find the meeting chat in your chat list and select Join​


IN A CHANNEL

To start an Instant Channel meeting: 

Go to Teams   on the left side of the app. Choose the channel you want to meet in from the list.​ 

In the Posts tab, go to where you type new messages (at the very bottom of the app) and select Meet now. Or, to keep the context of a specific conversation, choose Reply below any post, and then Meet now under the box where you'd type your message



Give your meeting a title and choose whether you want to include video. When you're ready, click Meet now.



Your meeting is now running, and anyone in the channel can join it. To Invite people to your meeting: 

Start typing the name of someone you want to invite in the box under People in the top right. Select them when they appear in the list, and they'll get a call right away.

https://creative.adobe.com/

To install additional Adobe Applications as part of your checked out Adobe Creative Cloud license:


1. If you've not done so already, Click the Accept Invitation link in your invitation email and setup an Adobe ID




2. Open https://creative.adobe.com/ , sign in, and click the Download Center link at the top of the page





 3. Scroll down the page to Creative Cloud and click Download


4. Once Creative Cloud downloads and installs, sign in with your Adobe ID



5. Click "Install or update an application"



6. Find the application you would like to install from the list and click Install

https://my.newforma.com/

iPhone

The app to download from the Apple App store is Newforma Capture. It is a multi-purpose app that allows the capture of several different types of content.



You will need to follow the instructions below to set up a Newforma ID account before you can sign into the Capture app.

Android

The app to download from the Google Play store is Newforma Field Notes.

You will need to follow the instructions below to set up a Newforma ID account before you can sign into the Field Notes app. 

The next step after downloading the app from either the Play Store (Android) or App Store (iPhone) will be to go to my.newforma.com and sign up for a new account. This will require you to enter a different username and password of your choosing. These are the credentials you will use to sign into the Newforma mobile apps. You will want to make sure and use your Gresham Smith email address to sign up for Newforma ID, so that you are identified as a subscriber.



After this step, you will receive an email to complete the process of setting up and connecting to Gresham Smith’s Info Exchange site. Upon clicking on the link, you will be taken to a page to set your password for your Newforma ID. After supplying that information, you will direct to the page where you will attach the Gresham Smith Info Exchange to your Newforma ID account. 

After selecting Gresham Smith from the list populated from your search, you will be seeing a disclaimer appear.

This will redirect you to the GS Info Exchange site, and require you to enter your network credentials (what you log into your work computer with) to access our Info Exchange portal. Please note that this is not the same credentials you have set up for your Newforma ID.

After you have successfully entered your Gresham Smith Info Exchange credentials, you will be redirected to a screen that will show you the projects you have access to.

When you see this screen, you have successfully connected to our Info Exchange through Newforma ID. From here you will use your Newforma ID to sign into the mobile apps and will have access to your projects. For further assistance, please feel free to reach out to Matt Freudenthal, your Newforma Administrator. ​​​​​​​

When you power on the device for the first time, choose your language and country...

Setup Manually

Choose "Use Cellular Connection" to activate the iPad's Cellular Data Plan.  This should take less than 5 minutes.  If it takes more than 15 minutes, please reach out to Graham Hamlin or James Amos.  Choose the Wi-Fi network you want to use if Cellular Data does not activate.



Next on the Remote Management

Sign in with your @greshamsmith.com email address.  If it does not work, use @gspnet.com email address. (Some accounts have not been swapped over on the backend)

Enable Location Services (this step is super important so we can locate the device in case it is misplaced)

Set your lock code

Wait on applications to come in.  Applications will start installing within 15 minutes. 

If there are additional applications that you require for the particular job, feel free to create an Apple account using your @greshamsmith email. Put in a ticket with Helpdesk if there are additional paid apps you require. We may have them already. 

Newforma is our current standard for site visits and markups.

Dimensions: 305x144

Outlook includes a Junk E-mail folder to prevent unwanted messages from reaching your Inbox. However, it is possible for important emails to be sent to the Junk E-mail folder unexpectedly. See the suggestions below for steps to prevent missing important communications.


  • Check your Junk E-mail folder regularly. Several filters are in place to prevent spam, phishing, and malware from reaching your Inbox. From time to time, one of these filters may send an important email to Junk E-Mail. This can happen even for emails sent from trusted contacts who you have communicated with in the past.​​​​​​​​​​​​​​ If there are spam or phishing emails in your Junk E-mail folder, these can be ignored - it means the filters are doing their job correctly.
  • If you discover an email in your Junk E-mail folder that should have been sent to your Inbox, right click it, go to Junk, and report it as "Not Junk". This will move it to your Inbox, and you'll be given an option to always trust emails from this sender. ***It may take some time for the filters to update, so you may have to do this multiple times for the same sender - another reason to regularly check your Junk E-mail folder.***


  • Messages delivered to the Junk E-mail folder will be permanently deleted after 30 days. The IT Department will be unable to recover emails once they've been deleted from the Junk E-mail folder, so be sure to check regularly for important messages and report them as Not Junk.

Microsoft Teams Meetings

Microsoft Teams Meetings can have 250 participants.  Meeting use Microsoft cloud services and not Gresham Smith resources.  You can view up to 4 participants cameras at a time, these are determined by most active audio.  You can Share desktop, applications, or even a Whiteboard.


Video Instructions by Microsoft? <- Clicky


Create a New Teams Meeting


From Outlook
  • From the Outlook Calendar, Select New Teams Meeting at the top.

  • Or Select New Items and Teams Meeting

  • Enter the Title, Required and Optional Attendees, Start time and End time, Location and in enter anything in the body above the ------


In Microsoft Teams
  • Open Microsoft Teams, Click Start button, and type teams then open Microsoft Teams.

  • Open the Calendar, on left hand side select Calendar.
  • Select New Meeting in top left corner
  • Enter Title, add Participants, add Optional Participants, Change Date and Time, Reoccurrence, add to a particular Teams Channel, Location and Details.
  • Select Save to create the Teams Meeting Invite.



Joining Teams Meetings


From Microsoft Teams
  • Open the Calendar in Microsoft Teams and find your meeting and open it and select Join Microsoft Teams Meeting.
  •  Or while in the Teams Meeting click the Join button if it has already started (Join button only shows during the meeting time slot).

From Outlook 
  • Open Meeting from calendar or from Meeting Notification and select Join Microsoft Teams meeting in body of meeting.





Meeting Options 





  • Camera - Turn camera on or off.
  • Blur - Once camera is one can turn on blur to blur background.
  • Microphone - Turn off Microphone.
  • Cogwheel - Select audio device.
  • Join Now - Join the Meeting.
Other Join Options
  • Audio off - Do not join Audio for meeting -> Select this option if using a conference room or cove equipment.
  • Phone audio - Have the meeting call another number for audio.
  • Add a room - Click drop down and choose Office Location Conference Rooms then select conference room you are in.


Teams Meeting Controls

  • Time - Duration of meeting.
  • Camera - Turn camera on or off.
  • Microphone - Mute and unmute microphone.
  • Share - Share content.
  • Dots - More options (see below).
  • Chat - Open chat window.
  • People - Participant list.
  • Hang up - Leave Meeting.
More Options
  • Show device settings - Change audio device.
  • Show meeting notes - Start meeting notes and save.
  • Show meeting details - Shows details of meeting.
  • Enter full screen - Enter and Exit full screen mode. 
  • Start video with blue - Turn on camera with blur.
  • Turn on live captions (preview) - Turn on closed captions.
  • Keypad - Bring up dial pad.
  • Start record - Start and stop meeting recording.
